# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-29 23:01:41.266282

### Base Program

```py
def total_area(ax1, ay1, ax2, ay2, bx1, by1, bx2, by2):
    area1 = (ax2 - ax1) * (ay2 - ay1)
    area2 = (bx2 - bx1) * (by2 - by1)

    overlap_width = min(ax2, bx2) - max(ax1, bx1)
    overlap_height = min(ay2, by2) - max(ay1, by1)

    overlap_area = max(overlap_width, 0) * max(overlap_height, 0)

    return area1 + area2 - overlap_area
```

### Input

```json
[1, 90, 73, 58, 68, 70, 89, 86]
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def total_area(ax1, ay1, ax2, ay2, bx1, by1, bx2, by2):
    area1 = (ax2 - ax1) * (ay2 - ay1)
    area2 = (bx2 - bx1) * (by2 - by1)
    overlap_width = min(ax2, bx2) - max(ax1, bx1)
    overlap_height = min(ay2, by2) - max(ay1, by1)
    overlap_area = max(overlap_width, 0) * max(overlap_height, 0)
    return area1 + area2 - overlap_area
```

<details>
<summary>parser endpoint: passed ✅</summary>

Message: 
```
Success
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def total_area(var_0, var_1, var_2, var_3, var_4, var_5, var_6, var_7):
    area1 = (var_2 - var_0) * (var_3 - var_1)
    area2 = (var_6 - var_4) * (var_7 - var_5)
    overlap_width = min(var_2, var_6) - max(var_0, var_4)
    overlap_height = min(var_3, var_7) - max(var_1, var_5)
    overlap_area = max(overlap_width, 0) * max(overlap_height, 0)
    return area1 + area2 - overlap_area
```

<summary>parser endpoint: passed ✅</summary>

```
Success
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def total_area(ax1, ay1, ax2, ay2, bx1, by1, bx2, by2):
    area1 = (ay2 + -ay1) * (ax2 + -ax1)
    area2 = (by2 + -by1) * (bx2 + -bx1)
    overlap_width = min(ax2, bx2) + -max(ax1, bx1)
    overlap_height = min(ay2, by2) + -max(ay1, by1)
    overlap_area = max(overlap_height, 0) * max(overlap_width, 0)
    return area2 + area1 + -overlap_area
```

<details>
<summary>parser endpoint: passed ✅</summary>

```
Success
```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def total_area(var_8, var_9, var_10, var_11, var_12, var_13, var_14, var_15):
    area1 = (var_11 + -var_9) * (var_10 + -var_8)
    area2 = (var_15 + -var_13) * (var_14 + -var_12)
    overlap_width = min(var_10, var_14) + -max(var_8, var_12)
    overlap_height = min(var_11, var_15) + -max(var_9, var_13)
    overlap_area = max(overlap_height, 0) * max(overlap_width, 0)
    return area2 + area1 + -overlap_area
```
